(Sections 504 and 514) Appendix F 
F-7 
Application of Funds and Accounts 
The Resolution provides that the proceeds of the Bonds, Revenues and other moneys 
deposited in the various funds and accounts under the Resolution shall be applied as follows (other 
than the Insurance Reserve Fund): 
Project Fund. Unless otherwise provided in th e Applicable Supplemental Resolution, the 
Commission shall establish within the Project F und a separate account (“Project Account”) for 
each Series of Bonds. Amounts in any Project Account shall be applied by the Commission to the 
Cost of Issuance of the Series of Bonds for whic h such Account was estab lished and to the Cost 
of the Projects financed in whole or in part by such Series. Upon completion of such Projects, the 
Commission is required to file a certificate with the Trustee, approved by a Consulting Engineer, 
setting forth the final Cost of such Projects and stating that such Projects have been completed to 
the satisfaction of the Commission and that all amounts withdrawn from the applicable Project 
Account for such Project, other th an amounts applied to the Cost of  Issuance, have been applied 
to the Cost of such Projects. Any balance remain ing in the Project Account not required to pay 
Costs of the Projects or Cost of Issuance shall be applied by the Commission at its discretion, to 
the Cost of Capital Improvements, including other Projects, by deposit of such amount in another 
and separate Project Account or Temporary Project Account or in the Renewal and Replacement 
Account or to the redemption of  the Bonds of the Series for which such Project Account was 
established by deposit of such amount in the applicable account in the Redemption Fund.   
Upon the determination by the Commission that a Project to be undertaken or undertaken 
has been or should be delayed and that no further amounts or significantly reduced amounts should 
be expended with respect thereto from the ap plicable Project Account, the Commission may, by 
resolution duly adopted by the Commission, elect to transfer amounts then on deposit in the 
applicable Project Account to (i) another and separate Project Account or to a Temporary Project 
Account or (ii) the applicable account in the Redemption Fund for application to the redemption 
of Bonds of the Series for whic h such Project Account was establ ished; provided, however, that 
the Commission shall also determine that any such  transfer will not impa ir the ability of the 
Commission to meet the requirements of the Revenue Fund during the next succeeding Fiscal Year 
based on the Annual Budget for such Fiscal Year. 
At any time that the Commission determines by resolution to undertake Capital 
Improvements to be financed in whole or in part by Bonds to be issued in the future, the 
Commission may establish within the Project F und one or more separate accounts (“Temporary 
Project Accounts”) for such Capital Improvements. Amounts in a Temporary Project Account shall 
be applied by the Commission to the Cost of the Capital Improvements for which such account 
was established. Upon the delivery of the first Series of Bonds issued in whole or in part to finance 
the Cost of such Capital Improve ments, any balance in a Temporary Project Account applicable 
to such Capital Improvements, unless otherw ise provided in the S upplemental Resolution 
authorizing such Series, shall be withdrawn and deposited in the applicab le Project Account for 
such Series.

and Maintenance Fund shall be applied by the Commission from time to time to Operating

Replacement Account shall be applied to the Cost of Capital Improvements to be financed in whole 
or in part from such Account as provided in the applicable Capital Improvements Budget described

Senior Debt Service Fund. Amounts in the Senior  Debt Service Fund shall be applied to

Payment may, and if so directed by the Commission shall, be appl ied by the Trustee prior to the

of the Series and maturity for which such Sink ing Fund Payment was esta blished, at prices not 
exceeding the applicable sinking fund Redemption Price plus interest, or to the redemption of such 
Senior Bonds then redeemable by their terms. As soon as practicable after the 45th day preceding 
the due date of any such Sinking Fund Payment, the Trustee shall call for redemption on such due 
date Senior Bonds of the Series and matu rity for which such Sinking Fund Payment was 
established in an amount sufficient to complete the retirement of the principal amount of the Senior 
Bonds of such Series and maturity as specified for such Sinking Fund Payment in the applicable 
Supplemental Resolution. Such call for redemption shall be made whether or not the balance in 
the Senior Debt Service Fund is su fficient to pay all such Senior Bonds. In satisfaction, in whole 
or in part, of any Sinking Fund Payment, there may be delivered on behalf of the Commission to 
the Trustee at any time up to 45 days prior to the due date of any Sinking Fund Payment Senior 
Bonds of the Series and maturity entitled to such  payment. All Senior Bonds so delivered to the 
Trustee shall reduce the amount of the Sinking F und Payment by the amount of the aggregate of 
the sinking fund Redemption Prices of such Senior Bonds.  
(Sections 506 (1) – 506(3))

Amounts accumulated in the Subordinated Debt Service Fund with respect to any Sinking

Commission, shall, be applied by the Trustee prior to the 45th day preceding the due date of such 
Sinking Fund Payment, to the purchase of Subordinated Bonds of the Series and maturity for which 
such Sinking Fund Payment was established, at pr ices not exceeding the applicable sinking fund 
Redemption Price plus interest, or to the redemption of such Subordinated Bonds then redeemable 
by their terms. As soon as practicable after the 45th day preceding the due date of any such Sinking 
Fund Payment, the Trustee shall call for redemp tion on such due date Subordinated Bonds of the 
Series and maturity for which such Sinking Fund Payment was established in an amount sufficient 
to complete the retirement of the principal amount of the Subordinated Bonds of such Series and Appendix F 
F-9 
maturity as specified for such Sinking Fund Payment in the Applicable Supplemental Resolution. 
Such call for redemption shall be made whether or not the balance in the Subordinated Debt 
Service Fund is sufficient to pay all such Subordinated Bonds. In satisfaction, in whole or in part, 
of any Sinking Fund Payment, there may be delivered on behalf of the Commission to the Trustee 
at any time up to 45 days prior to the due date of any Sinking Fund Payment Subordinated Bonds 
of the Series and maturity entitled to such paym ent. All Subordinated Bonds so delivered to the

(Section 511) 
Redemption Fund. The Commission may deposit in the Redemption Fund any moneys, 
including Revenues, not otherwise required by th e Resolution to be deposited or applied. There 
shall be established in the Redemption Fund a “Senior Redemp tion Account” with respect to 
Senior Bonds and a “Subordinated Redemption A ccount” with respect to Subordinated Bonds. 
Amounts in the applicable account in the Redemption Fund may be applied by the Commission to 
the optional redemption of Senior Bonds or Subordinated Bonds or to the purchase of Senior Bonds 
or Subordinated Bonds at prices not exceeding th e applicable Redemption Prices (plus accrued 
interest) had such Bonds been redeemed.  
(Section 507) 
Operating Reserve Fund. If at any time the amount on deposit and available therefor in the 
Senior Debt Service Fund, Redemption Fund, Stab ilization Fund, Senior Debt Service Reserve 
Fund, Renewal and Replacement Reserve Fund and Renewal and Replacement Account is 
insufficient to pay the principal and Redemption Pr ice of and interest on the Senior Bonds then 
due, the Trustee shall transfer from the Operating Reserve Fund to the Senior Debt Service Fund 
the amount necessary to meet the deficiency. If at any time the amount on deposit and available 
therefor in the Subordinated Debt Service Fund, Subordinated Redemption Account, Stabilization 
Fund, Subordinated Debt Service Reserve Fund,  Renewal and Replacement Reserve Fund and 
Renewal and Replacement Account is insufficient to pay the pr incipal and Redemption Price of 
and interest on the Subordinated Bonds then due, the Trustee, subject to any withdrawals required 
to be made by the preceding sentence, shall tr ansfer from the Operating Reserve Fund to the 
Subordinated Debt Service Fund the amount necessa ry to meet the deficiency. Subject to any 
withdrawals required purs uant to the previous tw o sentences, (i) if at any time the amount on 
deposit in the Operating Account is  insufficient to pay all Operati ng Expenses then payable, the 
Trustee shall withdraw from the Operating Re serve Fund and pay to the Commission for deposit 
in the Operating Account the amount  of the deficiency, and (ii) if  on any due date of an MWRA 
Assessment the amount on deposit in the MDC Assessments Fund is insufficient to pay the MWRA 
Assessment then due, the Trustee will withdraw from the Operating Reserve Fund and deposit in 
the MDC Assessments Fund the amount of the deficiency.  
(Section 508) 
Stabilization Fund. Amounts shall be deposited into the Stabilization Fund as provided in 
a Supplemental Resolution. The Fourth Supplemen tal Resolution provides that the Commission 
may request in writing that deposits in excess of  the Stabilization Fund  Requirement (defined Appendix F 
F-10 
below) be made to the Stabil ization Fund, provided that at th e time of such deposits all 
requirements for the funding of all funds and accounts established under the Resolution shall be 
satisfied. The Seventh Supplemen tal Resolution requires that upon the issuance of any Variable 
Rate Bonds containing provisions for interest rate changes on an annual basis or more frequently, 
the “Stabilization Fund Requireme nt” shall consist of an amount equal to four percent of the 
principal amount of any Variable Rate Bonds Outstanding. Any additional required amount 
resulting from the issuance of Variable Rate B onds shall be funded monthly to provide for the 
deposit of one percent of the original principal amount of such additional Variable Rate Bonds in 
each Fiscal Year until the additional required amount is on deposit in the Stabilization Fund.  
If the amount on deposit in the Stabilization Fund is at least equal to the Stabilization Fund 
Requirement, all or a portion of the amounts on deposit therein may be transferred to the Revenue 
Fund. If on the last day of any Fiscal Year subsequent to the initial funding period relating to any 
Variable Rate Bonds, the amount on deposit in the Stabilization Fund is less than the Stabilization 
Fund Requirement, additional monthly deposits will be made into the Stabilization Fund from the 
Revenue Fund in the next succeeding Fiscal Year  equal to one-twelfth (1/12th) of one-eighth 
(1/8th) of the Stabilization Fund Requirement until the amounts on deposit therein are equal to the 
Stabilization Fund Requirement. 
In accordance with the above provisions in the Seventh Supplemental Resolution, the Tenth 
Supplemental Resolution establishes an additional  Stabilization Fund Requi rement equal to four 
percent of the principal amount of the 1994 Series A Bonds. 
(Section 509) 
Senior Debt Service Reserve Fund. If at a ny time the amounts on deposit and available 
therefor in the Senior Debt Service Fund, the Redemption Fund and the Stabilization Fund are 
insufficient to pay the principal and the Redemption Price of and interest on the Senior Bonds then 
due, the Trustee shall withdraw from the Senior  Debt Service Reserve Fund and deposit in the 
Senior Debt Service Fund the amount necessary to meet the deficiency. Amounts so withdrawn 
shall be derived, first, from cas h or Permitted Invest ments on deposit ther ein and, second, from 
draws or demands on Reserve Requirements held as a part thereof upon the terms and conditions 
set forth in any such Reserve Requirement or as  set forth in the Supplemental Resolution setting 
forth such Reserve Requirement. If on the last business day of  any month the amount on deposit 
in the Senior Debt Service Reserve Fund is in excess of the Senior Funded Debt Service Fund 
Requirement, the Trustee will withdraw such excess and deposit it in the Revenue Fund.  
(Section 510).  
Subordinated Debt Service Reserve Fund. If at any time the am ount on deposit and 
available therefor in the Subordinated Debt Service Fund, Subordinated Redemption Account and 
the Stabilization Fund is insufficient to pay the principal and Redemption Price of and interest on 
the Subordinated Bonds then due, the Trustee shall withdraw from the Subordinated Debt Service 
Reserve Fund the amount necessary to meet th e deficiency. Amounts so withdrawn shall be 
derived, first, from cash or Perm itted Investments on deposit therein and, second, from draws or 
demands on Reserve Requirements held as a part thereof upon th e terms and conditions set forth 
in any such Reserve Requirement or as set forth in the Supplemental Resolution setting forth such Appendix F 
F-11 
Reserve Requirement. If on the last business day of any month the amount on deposit in the 
Subordinated Debt Service Reserv e Fund is in excess of the S ubordinated Funded Debt Service 
Reserve Fund Requirement, the Trustee will with draw such excess and deposit it in the Revenue 
Fund.  
(Section 512) 
MDC Assessments Fund. Amounts in the MD C Assessments Fund shall, subject to 
transfers to the Senior Debt Service Fund and Subordinated Debt Service Fund, be applied to the 
payment of MWRA Assessments on the due dates thereof. 
(Section 514) 
Renewal and Replacement Reserve Fund. If at any time the amounts on deposit and 
available therefor in the Seni or Debt Service Fund, Redempti on Fund, Stabiliz ation Fund and 
Senior Debt Service Reserve Fund are insufficient to pay the pr incipal and Redemption Price of 
and interest on the Senior Bonds then due, th e Trustee shall transfer from the Renewal and 
Replacement Reserve Fund to the Senior Debt Serv ice Fund the amount necessary to meet the 
deficiency. If at any time the amounts on deposit and available therefor in the Subordinated Debt 
Service Fund, Subordinated Redemption Account,  Stabilization Fund and Subordinated Debt 
Service Reserve Fund are insufficient to pay the principal and Redemption Price of and interest on 
the Subordinated Bonds then due, the Trustee, subject to any withdrawals required by the 
preceding sentence, shall transfer from the Renewal and Replacement Reserve Fund to the 
Subordinated Debt Service Fund the amount necessa ry to meet the deficiency. Subject to any 
withdrawals required pursuant to the previous two sentences, the Commission may apply amounts 
in the Renewal and Replacement Reserve Fund solely to the Cost of any Capital Improvement the 
cost of which, if moneys were available therefor, could be paid from the Renewal and Replacement 
Account in accordance with the Resolution. The Trustee shall pay from such Fund to the 
Commission for deposit in the Renewal and Re placement Account any amount requested by the 
Commission but only upon receipt of a certificate specifying the Capital Improvement to which 
such amount will be applied, its estimated Cost  and estimated completion date and certifying, 
among other things, that such Capital Improvement  is reasonably required for the continued 
operation of the System or the maintenance of Revenues. 
(Section 515) 
General Fund. Amounts on deposit in the General Fund may be held and applied by the 
Commission to any use or purpose of the Co mmission. In addition to amounts specifically 
provided or permitted by the Resolution to be deposited in the General Fund, the Commission may 
deposit therein any other moneys received from any source unless such moneys are required to be 
otherwise applied by the Resolution. 
(Section 516) 
Application of Funds and Accounts in the Event of Insufficient Revenue 
If on any due date of Principal Installments or interest on the Senior Bonds the amount on 
deposit in the Senior Debt Service Fund is insufficient to make the required payments in full, the 
Trustee will withdraw from the following funds and accounts and in the following order amounts Appendix F 
F-12 
sufficient to satisfy the deficiency: (1) Redemption Fund; (2) Stabilization Fund; (3) Senior Debt 
Service Reserve Fund; (4) Renewal and Re placement Reserve Fund; (5) Renewal and 
Replacement Account; (6) Operating Reserve Fund; (7) Insurance Reserve Fund; (8) Subordinated 
Debt Service Fund; (9) MDC Assessments Fund. 
If on any due date of Principal Installments or interest on the Subordinated Bonds the 
amount on deposit in the Subordinated Debt Servic e Fund is insufficient to make the required 
payments in full, the Trustee will withdraw from the following funds and accounts and in the 
following order amounts sufficient to satisf y the deficiency: (1) Subordinated Redemption 
Account; (2) Stabilization Fund; (3) Subordinated Debt Service Reserve Fund; (4) Renewal and 
Replacement Reserve Fund; (5) Renewal and Replacement Account; (6) Operating Reserve Fund; 
(7) Insurance Reserve Fund; (8) MDC Assessments Fund. 
(Sections 505, 507, 508, 509, 510, 511, 514 and 515) 
Investments and Deposits 
Except as otherwise provided below and in th e Resolution, money held  for the credit of 
any fund or account under the Resolution shall be i nvested by the Trustee at the direction of the 
Commission in Permitted Investments which shall mature or be redeemable at the option of the 
holder thereof on such dates and in such amounts as may be necessary to provide moneys to meet 
the payments from such funds and accounts. Notwithstanding the foregoing, moneys in either the 
Senior Debt Service Reserve Fund or the Subo rdinated Debt Service Reserve Fund shall be 
invested solely in the investment s specified in paragraphs (i), (i i) and (viii) of the definition of 
Permitted Investments. Permitted Investments purchased as an investment of moneys in any fund 
or account shall be deemed at all times to be a part of such fund or account and all income thereon 
shall accrue to and be deposited in such fund or account and all losses from investment shall be 
charged against such fund or account; provided th at all income earned on investment of the 
Operating Reserve Fund, Renewal and Replacement Reserve Fund, MDC Assessments Fund, City 
Bond Fund, the Insurance Reserve Fund, the Stab ilization Fund and, if  authorized by the 
Applicable Supplemental Resolu tion, the Project Account for an y Series of Bonds, shall be 
credited to and deposited in the Revenue Fund. 
In lieu of investment in Pe rmitted Investments, amounts on deposit in the Operating and 
Maintenance Fund, in the General Fund, in any Project Account or Temporary Project Account in 
the Project Fund or in the In surance Reserve Fund may be deposited by the Commission on 
demand or on time deposit with such depositori es as the Commission may from time to time 
appoint for such purpose. Any depository so appointed shall be a bank or trust company which is 
a member of the Federal Depos it Insurance Corporation orga nized under the laws of the 
Commonwealth or a national banking association authorized to do business in, and having its 
principal office in, the Commonwealth and in each case qualified under the laws of the 
Commonwealth to receive deposits  of public moneys. No moneys  shall be deposited with a 
depository in amounts in excess of Federal Deposit Insurance Corporation insurance limits unless 
such depository has a combined capital and surplus of at least $50,000,000. All moneys so 
deposited shall be secured to the extent and in  the manner required by law for the securing of 
deposits of a city in the Commonwealth. 
(Section 517) Appendix F 
F-13 
Holding of Special Deposits 
Moneys held by or for the account of the Co mmission which are required to be applied 
under the terms of an agreement to the construction or alteration of a facility or which are subject 
to refund by the Commission or held for the account  of others or subject to refund to others, 
including, without limitation, any amounts which, under any ag reement by the Commission 
providing for adequate separation of such amounts from Revenues, are collected by the 
Commission on behalf of others for services rendered or commodities provided to customers, any 
amounts deducted by the Commission from wage and sa lary payments to th e employees of the 
Commission, and amounts contributed by the Commis sion to any pension or retirement fund or 
system, which amounts are held in trust for the benefit of the employees of the Commission, and 
any amounts held as deposits, including customers’ service deposits, guaranteed revenue contract 
deposits, unexpended developers’ deposits under construction loan contracts, minimum revenue 
deposits and unexpended jobbing deposits, together with any investments of such moneys and 
interest and profits thereon, ma y be held by the Commission outside of the various funds and 
accounts established by the Resolu tion and shall not be subject to the pledge created by the 
Resolution or be considered Revenues thereunder while so held. 
(Section 518) 
Covenant as to Rates and Charges 
So long as any Bonds are Outstanding, the Commission is required to establish and 
maintain Rates and Charges adequate at all times, with other available funds, to provide Revenues 
and other moneys, including any Reserved Revenues directed by the Commission to be deposited 
in the Revenue Fund, at least sufficient, with such margin of safety as the Commission shall deem 
reasonable, to pay or provide for (a) all Opera ting Expenses and all MWRA Assessments, (b) all 
payments of principal, premium, if any, and interest on the Bonds and all other indebtedness of or 
assumed by the Commission, (c) all amounts payable to the Operating Reserve Fund, Senior Debt 
Service Reserve Fund, Subordinated Debt Se rvice Reserve Fund, Renewal and Replacement 
Reserve Fund and Insurance Reserve Fund, (d) all repairs, replacements and renewals of the 
System deemed necessary by the Commission and (e) all other amounts which the Commission 
may by law or contract be obligated to pay. 
Without limiting the generality of the fo regoing, the Commissi on is required by the 
Resolution to establish and maintain Rates and Ch arges at levels sufficient so that total Net 
Revenues in each Fiscal Year during which Bonds are outstanding shall equal at least one hundred 
twenty-five percent of (1) the Bond Debt Serv ice Requirement during such Fiscal Year with 
respect to all Bonds Outstanding as of the first day of such Fiscal Year less (2) the amount, if any, 
of Bond proceeds available to pay interest becoming due in such Fiscal Year on Bonds Outstanding 
as of the first day of such Fiscal Year. Failure by the Commission to comply with the requirements 
of the foregoing sentence shall not be considered an Event of Default under the Resolution so long 
as the Commission has complied or is diligently pr oceeding to comply with the requirements of 
the following paragraph. 
On or before the last day of each Fiscal Year the Commission must review the adequacy 
of its Rates and Charges to satisfy the foregoing rate covenant for the next succeeding Fiscal Year. Appendix F 
F-14 
If such review, or any report of a Consulting Engi neer required by the Resolution, indicates that 
the Rates and Charges are, or are likely to be, insufficient to meet such requirements, the 
Commission must promptly take such steps as ar e permitted by law and as are necessary to cure 
or avoid the deficiency. 
(Section 603) 
Covenant as to Budgets 
Not less than one day prior to the beginning of each Fiscal Year, the Commission is 
required to adopt and file with the Trustee an annual operating budget (“Annual Budget”) for such 
Fiscal Year and a final budget (“Capital Improvements Budget”) for the Capital Improvements or 
parts thereof to be undertaken by the Commission in such Fiscal Year. The Commission may at 
any time, but not more often than once a month, file with the Trustee an amended or supplemental 
Annual Budget or Capital Improvements Budget for the Fiscal Year then in progress. The Annual 
Budget is required to show fo r each month projected Operati ng Expenses and the projected 
amounts to be deposited in and withdrawn from each of the funds and accounts under the 
Resolution in each month and the Revenues projec ted to be available to meet the same. The 
Commission shall not incur aggregate Operating Expenses in any Fiscal Year in excess of the 
aggregate amount of Operatin g Expenses shown in the A nnual Budget as amended and 
supplemented for such Fiscal Year except in case of emergency or as required by law. The Capital 
Improvements Budget shall be prepared on the basi s of monthly requirements and shall show for 
each month required disbursements from the Renewal and Replacement Account, from any Project 
Account or Temporary Project Ac count in the Project Fund and, to  the extent provided by the 
Commission, any other fund or account under the Resolution as well as the sources of moneys 
projected to be available to meet the same. The Capital Improvements Budget shall further identify 
the Capital Improvements to be undertaken, the nature of the work, the estimated Cost thereof, and 
the estimated completion date of each Capital Improvement. 
Not later than the last day of Fiscal Year 1987 and each third full Fiscal Year thereafter, 
the Commission shall cause an ex amination of and report on the properties and operations of the 
System to be made by a Consulting Engineer and shall cause a copy of such examination and report 
to be filed with the Trustee. Such examinati on and report shall include a review of, among other 
things, the Commission’s then current three year Capital Improvement program, the current and 
any proposed Capital Improvements Budget and A nnual Budget and such other reports as the 
Commission shall deem necessary. Any report prepared by the Consulting Engineer in connection 
with the issuance of Additional Bonds within such three year period shall satisfy the requirements 
of this subsection for such three year period. 
(Sections 607 and 608) 
Covenant with Respect to Creation of Liens and Other Indebtedness 
The Commission may not issue any indebtedness, other than the Bonds, secured by a 
pledge of or other lien on th e Revenues and other moneys, securities and funds under the 
Resolution, and may not otherwise create any lien or charge on such Revenues, moneys, securities 
and funds, except as follows: Appendix F 
F-15 
The Commission may at any time issue notes  or other evidence of indebtedness (and 
renewals thereof): 
(a) in anticipation of the issue of Bonds, which notes, if so determined by the 
Commission, may be secured by a pledge  of the proceeds of the Bonds in 
anticipation of which such notes are issued and by a pledge of Revenues, provided 
that such pledge of Revenues must be subordinate to the pledge created by the 
Resolution; 
(b) in anticipation of grant receipts from th e United States or the Commonwealth or 
any agency, instrumentality or political subdivision of either for Capital 
Improvements and payable solely out of, or secured by a pledge of the amounts to 
be received; provided that no such notes may be issued unless the Commission has 
received an executed agreement for the grant, the aggregate amount of such notes 
may not exceed the amount of the grant not  yet received and all such notes or 
renewals thereof must mature not later than the expected date of receipt of such 
grant; or 
(c) in anticipation of the Revenues to be received in any Fiscal Year, which notes may 
be payable out of, or secured by a pledge of, Revenues; provided that such pledge 
must be subordinate to the pledge creat ed by the Resolution, any such notes or 
renewals thereof issued in a Fiscal Year must be payable within such Fiscal Year, 
the aggregate principal amount of such notes outstanding at any one time in a Fiscal 
Year may not exceed fifty percent of the Revenues for the immediately preceding 
Fiscal Year, and the proceeds of such not es (other than the proceeds of renewal 
notes required to pay notes) must be deposited in the Revenue Fund. 
The Commission may also incur indebtedne ss secured by moneys derived by the 
Commission from the lease, license, operation, sale  or other disposition of any facility or 
equipment (whether or not part of the System) constructed or acquired by or on behalf of the 
Commission subsequent to the adoption of the Reso lution with the proceeds of such debt. Such 
moneys shall not be considered Revenues or Rates and Charges under the Resolution provided that 
neither the debt service on such indebtedness nor any cost of the acquisition, construction, 
operation, maintenance or repair of any such facility or equipment may be paid from the proceeds 
of Bonds or from Revenues (other than Revenue s deposited in the General Fund pursuant to the 
Resolution) or included in Operating Expenses and any such moneys in excess of such debt service 
and cost of acquisition, constructio n, operation, maintenance and repa ir must be deposited in the 
Revenue Fund (and upon such deposit shall be deemed  Revenues). Prior to the issue of any such 
indebtedness the Commission must deliver to th e Trustee a certificate of a Consulting Engineer 
stating that the lease, license, operation, sale or other disposition of such facility or equipment and 
the application of the moneys derived therefrom to the operation, maintenance and repair thereof 
and the payment of the debt service on the indebtedness issued therefor will not result in any 
decrease in the Net Revenues of the Commission during the succeeding five Fiscal Years. 
The Resolution also permits the Commission to  issue indebtedness which is payable out 
of, or secured by a pledge of, Revenues to be deri ved on or after such date  as the pledge of the 
Revenues created by the Resolution has been discharged as provided in the Resolution or which is Appendix F 
F-16 
payable solely out of, or secured solely by a pl edge of, amounts which ma y be deposited in the 
General Fund pursuant to the Resolution, provided  that the pledge of such amounts must be 
subordinate to the provisions of the Resolution. 
(Section 209) 
Events of Default; Acceleration of Maturities 
The Resolution declares the following to be “Events of Default” thereunder: 
(i) default in the payment of the principal or Redemption Price of any Bond when due, 
whether at maturity or by call for mandatory redemption or redemption at the option 
of the Commission or any registered owner, or otherwise, or in the payment of any 
Sinking Fund Payment when due; 
(ii) default in the payment of any installment of interest on any Bond when due; 
(iii) default by the Commission in the performance or observance of the covenant as to 
rates and charges provided in the Resolu tion and further the Commission fails to 
take steps diligently to remedy such de fault (see “Covenant as to Rates and 
Charges” above); 
(iv) default by the Commission in the perfo rmance or observance of any other 
covenants on its part provide d in the Resolution or in the Bonds and such default 
continues for a period of 30 days after receipt of written notice from the Trustee or 
the registered owners of a majority in  principal amount of the Senior Bonds 
Outstanding or, if no Senior Bonds are Outstanding, a majority in principal amount 
of Subordinated Bonds Outstanding; prov ided that if such default cannot be 
remedied within such 30-day period, it shal l not constitute an Event of Default if 
corrective action is instituted by the Commission within such period and diligently 
pursued until the default is remedied; 
(v) entrance by a court of compet ent jurisdiction, under the provision of any law for 
the relief of debtors, of an order, judgment or decree appointing a receiver, trustee, 
or liquidator for the Commission or the whole or any substantial part of the System, 
granting relief in involuntary proceedi ngs with respect to the Commission under 
the federal bankruptcy act, or assuming custody or control of the Commission or of 
the whole or any substantial part of the System, and the order, judgment or decree 
is not set aside or stayed within 60 days  from such date of entry of the order, 
judgment or decree; or 
(vi) the Commission admits in writing its inabi lity to pay its debts generally as they 
become due, commences voluntary proc eedings in bankruptcy or seeking a 
composition of indebtedness, makes an assi gnment for the benefit of its creditors, 
consents to the appointment of a receiver of the whole or any substantial part of the 
System under any law for the relief of debtors, or consents to the assumption by 
any court of competent jurisdiction unde r any law for the relief of debtors of 
custody or control of the Commission or of the whole or any substantial part of the 
System. Appendix F 
F-17 
Upon the occurrence of an Even t of Default and so long as the Event of Default is not 
cured, either the Trustee or the registered owners of twenty-five percent in principal amount of the 
Senior Bonds Outstanding or, if  no Senior Bonds are Outstand ing, of twenty-five percent in 
principal amount of the Subordina ted Bonds Outstanding, may decl are the principal of all the 
Bonds then Outstanding, and the interest accrued thereon, to be due and payable immediately. 
(Section 701) 
Application of Revenues and Other Moneys After Default 
The Commission covenants that if an Event of  Default occurs and is not remedied, the 
Commission, upon demand of the Trustee, shall pay over to the Trustee all moneys, securities and 
funds then held by the Commission in any fund or account pledged under the Resolution, and, as 
promptly as practicable after recei pt thereof, the Revenues. Subject to the pledges created by the 
Resolution, during the continuance of an Event of Default, the Trustee will apply the Revenues as 
follows and in the following order: 
(i) to the payment of the reasonable and proper charges and expenses of the Trustee and 
of any engineer or firm of engineers selected by the Trustee pursuant to the Resolution; 
(ii) to the payment of reasonable and necessary Operating Expenses, including reserve and 
working capital therefor and repair and replacement of the System necessary to prevent 
loss of Revenues or to provide  for the continued operation of  the System, as certified 
to the Trustee by an independent engineer or firm of engineers of recognized standing 
selected by the Trustee; 
(iii) to the payment of the interest and principal or Redemption Price then due on the Senior 
Bonds as follows: 
(a) unless the principal amount of all of the Senior Bonds has become 
or has been declared due and payable, 
First:  To the payment of all instal lments of interest then due in the 
order of the maturity of such installments, and, if the amount 
available is not sufficient to pay in full all installments maturing on 
the same date, then to the payment thereof ratably, without any 
discrimination or preference; and 
Second:  To the payment of th e unpaid principal amount or 
Redemption Price of any Senior Bonds which have become due, 
whether at maturity or  by call for redemption, in the order of their 
due dates, and, if the amount available is not sufficient to pay in full 
all the Senior Bonds due on any da te, then to the payment thereof 
ratably, without any discrimination or preference; and 
(b) if the principal of all of the Seni or Bonds has beco me or has been 
declared due and payable, to the payment of the principal amount 
and interest then due and unpaid  upon the Senior Bonds without Appendix F 
F-18 
preference or priority of principal over interest or of interest over 
principal, or of any installment of interest over any other installment 
of interest, or of any Senior Bond over any other Senior Bond, 
ratably, without any discrimination or preference; and 
(iv) the payment of the interest and princi pal or Redemption Price then due on the 
Subordinated Bonds, as follows: 
(a) unless the principal amount of a ll of the Subordinated Bonds has 
become or has been declared due and payable, 
First: To the payment of all installments of interest then due in the 
order of the maturity of such installments, and, if the amount 
available is not sufficient to pay in full all installments maturing on 
the same date, then to the payment thereof ratably, without any 
discrimination or preference; and  
Second: To the payment of th e unpaid principal amount or 
Redemption Price of any Subordinated Bonds which have become 
due, whether at maturity or by ca ll for redemption, in the order of 
their due dates, and, if the amount available is not sufficient to pay 
in full all the Subordinated Bonds  due on any date, then to the 
payment thereof ratably, according to the amounts of principal or 
Redemption Price due on such date , without any discrimination or 
preference; and 
(b) if the principal of all of the Subordinated Bonds has become or has 
been declared due and payable, to the payment of the principal 
amount and interest then due and unpaid upon the Subordinated 
Bonds without preference or priority of principal over interest or of 
interest over principal, or of a ny installment of interest over any 
other installment of interest, or of any Subordinated Bond over any 
other Subordinated Bond, ratably, without any discrimination or 
preference. 
Any amounts on deposit in the Subordinated Debt Service Reserve Fund shall not be 
applied as set forth above to th e payment of principal amount a nd interest on Senior Bonds and 
any amounts on deposit in the Senior Debt Service Fund, the Senior Redemption Account and the 
Senior Debt Service Reserve Fund shall not be a pplied as set forth above to the payment of the 
principal amount and interest on Subordinated Bonds. 
The proceeds of any Additional Security sha ll be applied by the Trustee in the manner 
provided in the Applicable Supplemental Resolution authorizing such Additional Security. 
(Section 702) 
  Appendix F 
F-19 
Proceedings Brought by Trustee 
Whether or not the principal of the Bonds, and the accrued interest thereon, is declared due 
and payable immediately, if an Event of Default occurs and is not remedied, the Trustee may 
proceed to protect and enforce its rights and the rights of the registered owners of the Bonds under 
the Resolution by suits in equity or at law, whether for the specific performance of any covenant, 
or in aid of the execution of any power granted, or for an accounting against the Commission as if 
the Commission were the trustee of an express trus t, or for the enforcement of any other right as 
the Trustee deems most effectual to enforce any of its rights or to perform any of its duties under 
the Resolution. Upon the occurrence of an Event of Default, the Trustee will also be entitled to 
obtain the appointment of a rece iver of the moneys, securitie s and funds then held by the 
Commission in any fund or account under the Reso lution and of the Revenues and the whole or 
any part of the System. During any period in whic h an Event of Default shall have occurred and 
be continuing, if there are any Outstanding Subordinated Bonds and Senior Bonds, the registered 
owners of the Subordinated Bonds shall be entitled  to the appointment of a trustee to act on their 
behalf in any suit, action or proceeding under the Resolution and to otherwise exercise on their 
behalf any of their rights under the Resolution, provi ded that such trustee is not entitled to hold 
any Funds or Accounts continued to be held by th e Trustee. Any such appointment may be made 
with the consent of a majority in principal amount Outstanding of Subordinated Bonds. 
(Section 703) 
Restriction on Bondholders’ Action 
No registered owner of any Bond has any right  to institute any suit,  action or proceeding 
at law or in equity for the enforcement of any provision of the Resolution or for any remedy under 
the Resolution, unless such registered owner has previously given to the Trustee written notice of 
the occurrence of an Event of Default and the registered owners of at least twenty-five percent in 
principal amount of the Bonds then Outstanding file a written request with the Trustee and offer it 
reasonable opportunity to exercise  the powers granted in the Re solution in its own name, and 
unless such registered owners o ffer to the Trustee adequate secu rity and indemnity against the 
costs, expenses and liabilities to be incurred thereby, and the Trustee refuses to comply with such 
request within a reasonable time. 
(Section 704) 
Defeasance 
If the Commission pays or causes to be paid, or there shall otherwise be paid, to the 
registered owners of the Bonds then Outstanding the principal amount and interest and Redemption 
Price, if any, to become due on all Outstanding Bonds, at the times and in the manner stipulated in 
the Bonds and in the Resolution, then the pledge of any Revenues or other moneys and securities 
and all other rights granted by the Resolution sha ll be discharged and satisfied. All Outstanding 
Bonds of any Series shall prior to the maturity or redemption date thereof be deemed to have been 
paid within the meaning of the foregoing sentence if, among other things, there has been deposited 
with the Trustee either moneys in a sufficient amount or Defeasance Obligations, the principal of 
and interest on which when due will provide moneys which shall be sufficient to pay when due Appendix F 
F-20 
the principal or Redemption Price, if applicable, and interest due and to become due on said Bonds 
on and prior to the redemption date or maturity date thereof, as the case may be. 
For purposes of determining whether Variable Rate Bonds shall be deemed to have been paid prior 
to the maturity or redemption date thereof, as the case may be, by the deposit of moneys, or 
Defeasance Obligations and moneys, if any, the interest to come due on such Variable Rate Bonds 
on or prior to the maturity date or redemption date thereof, as the case may be, shall be calculated 
at the Variable Rate Ceiling. 
Tender Bonds shall be deemed to have been paid only if, in addition to satisfying the requirements 
above, there shall have been deposited with th e Trustee moneys in an  amount which shall be 
sufficient to pay when due the maximum amount of principal of and premium, if any, and interest 
on such Bonds which could become  payable to the registered owners of such Bonds upon the 
exercise of any options provided to the registered owners of such Bonds; provided, however, that 
if, at the time a deposit is made with the Trustee the options originally exercisable by the registered 
owners of Tender Bonds are no longer exercisabl e, such Bonds shall not be considered Tender 
Bonds for purposes of this sentence.

FORM OF 
CONTINUING DISCLOSURE AGREEMENT 
THIS CONTINUING DISCLOSURE AGREEMENT dated as of July 7, 2021 (this “Agreement”) 
by and between the Boston Water and Sewer Commi ssion (the “Commission”), a body politic and 
corporate and a political subdivision of The Commonwealth of Massachusetts established by Chapter 436 
of the Acts of 1977 of the Commonwealth, as amende d (the “Enabling Act”), and U.S. Bank National 
Association, as dissemination agent (the “Dissemi nation Agent”) for the Commission’s General Revenue 
and Refunding Bonds (Senior Series), 2021 Series A (Gr een Bonds) (Federally Taxable), to be issued by 
the Commission in an aggregate principal amount of $157,710,000 (the “2021A Bonds”) and its General 
Revenue and Refunding Bonds (Senior Series), 2021 Series B, to be issued by the Commission in an 
aggregate principal amount of $40,630,000 (the “2 021B Bonds” and, collectively with the 2021A Bonds, 
the “2021 Bonds”). 
W I T N E S S E T H: 
WHEREAS, the Commission intends to issue the 2021A Bonds under and pursuant to (i) the 
Enabling Act (ii) the Commission’s General Revenue B ond Resolution adopted on  December 6, 1984, as 
amended and supplemented, (iii) the Commission’s Am ended and Restated Twenty-Eighth Supplemental 
Resolution adopted as of March 24, 2021 and (iv) the Commission’s Issuance Resolution adopted on 
March 24, 2021; 
WHEREAS, the Commission intends to issue the 2021B Bonds under and pursuant to (i) the 
Enabling Act (ii) the Commission’s General Revenue B ond Resolution adopted on  December 6, 1984, as 
amended and supplemented, (iii) the Commission’s Am ended and Restated Twenty-Ninth Supplemental 
Resolution adopted as of March 24, 2021 and (iv) the Commission’s Issuance Resolution adopted on 
March 24, 2021; 
WHEREAS, on November 10, 1994 the Securities and Exchange Commission (the “SEC”) 
adopted Release Number 34-34961 whic h amended Rule 15c2-12 (as define d herein), originally adopted 
by the SEC on June 28, 1989; 
WHEREAS, Rule 15c2-12 requires that prior to acting as a broker, dealer or municipal securities 
dealer (the “Participating Underwriter”) for the Commission’s 2021 Bonds, a Pa rticipating Underwriter 
must comply with the provisions of Rule 15c2-12; and  
WHEREAS, Rule 15c2-12 further provides, among other things, that a Pa rticipating Underwriter 
shall not purchase or sell the Commission’s 2021 B onds unless the Participating Underwriter has 
reasonably determined that the Commission and any “obligated person” (within the meaning of Rule 
15c2-12, as amended) have undertaken , either individually or in combination with others, in a written 
agreement for the benefit of Bondowners (as defined below), to provide certain information relating to the 
Commission, any “obligated person” and the 2021 Bonds, to the repositories described herein below.

 2. Definitions.  The following words and te rms used in this Agr eement shall have the 
following respective meanings: 
 
 “Bondowner” or “Owner” shall mean any regist ered owner of 2021 Bonds and any beneficial 
owner of 2021 Bonds who provides evidence satisfactory to the Trustee of such status. 
 
 “EMMA” means the MSRB’s Electronic Municipa l Market Access system, or its successor as 
designated by the MSRB; EMMA is available at emma.msrb.org 
 
 “MSRB” means the Municipal Securities Rulemaking Board.   
 
 “Official Statement” shall mean the Official Statement of the Commission, dated June 22, 2021, 
relating to the 2021 Bonds. 
 
 “Rule” or “Rule 15c2-12” shall mean Rule 15c 2-12 promulgated by the SEC under the Securities 
and Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (17 CFR Part 240 , §240.15c2-12), as in effect on the date of this 
Agreement, including any official interpretation thereof. 
 
 “SEC” shall mean the United Stat es Securities and Exchange Commission. 
 
 “State” or “Commonwealth” shall mean  The Commonwealth of Massachusetts. 
 
 All capitalized words and terms used in this Ag reement and not otherwi se defined herein shall 
have the meaning ascribed to such words and terms in  the Official Statement pertaining to the 2021 
Bonds. 
 
 3. The Undertaking of the Commission.   
 
 (a) The Commission hereby undertakes for the be nefit of the Bondowners to provide to the 
MSRB through its EMMA system, no later than 270 da ys after the end of each fiscal year of the 
Commission: (i) the annual financial information descr ibed below relating to such fiscal year, together 
with audited financial statements of the Commission for such fiscal year if audited financial statements 
are then available; provided, however, that if audite d financial statements of the Commission are not then 
available, unaudited financial statements shall be prov ided and such audited fina ncial statements shall be 
delivered to the MSRB through its EMMA system, when  they become available (but in no event later 
than 350 days after the end of such fiscal year); or  (ii) notice of the Commission’s failure, if any, to 
provide any such information.  The annual financial in formation to be provided shall consist of financial 
information and operating data, in  each case updated through the last day of such fiscal year unless 
otherwise noted, relating to the follo wing information contained in the Official Statement, and in each 
case substantially in the same level of detail as is found in the referenced section of the Official 
Statement:

related statements of revenue and cost of service a nd cash flows prepared in accordance with generally 
accepted accounting principles in effect from time to time.  Such financial statements shall be audited by 
a firm of certified public accountants appointed by the Commission.

 For the purposes of the event identified in subparagr aph (xii) above, the event is considered to occur 
when any of the following occur: the appointment of a receiver, fiscal agent or  similar officer for the 
obligated person in a proceeding under the U.S. Bankruptcy Code or in any other proceeding under state or 
federal law in which a court or governmental authority has assumed jurisdiction over substantially all of the 
assets or business of the obligated person, or if su ch jurisdiction has been assumed by leaving the existing 
governing body and officials or officers in possession but subject to the supervision and orders of a court or 
governmental authority, or the entry of an order confirming a plan of  reorganization, arrangement or 
liquidation by a court or governmental authority having supervision or jurisdiction over substantially all of 
the assets or business of the obligated person. 
 
 (c) Nothing in this Agreement shall pr eclude the Commission from disseminating any 
information in addition to that required hereunder.  If the Commission disseminates any such additional 
information, nothing in this Agreement shall oblig ate the Commission to update such information or to 
include it in any future materials disseminated. 
 
 4. Enforceability of This Agreement; Termina tion.  To the extent permitted by law, the 
provisions of this Agreement are enforceable ag ainst the Commission in acco rdance with the terms 
 
* As noted in Rule 15c2-12, the term “financial obligation”  means (i) a debt obligation, (ii) a derivative instrument 
entered into in connection with, or pledged as security or a source of payment for, an existing or planned debt 
obligation or (iii) a guaranty of an instrument described in  (i) or (ii). The term does not include municipal securities 
as to which a final official statement has been provided to the MSRB consistent with Rule 15c2-12.   Appendix G

thereof by any owner of a Bond, including any benefi cial owner acting as a third party beneficiary (upon 
proof of its status as a beneficial owner reasonabl y satisfactory to the Dissemination Agent).  To the 
extent permitted by law, any such owner shall have the right, for the equal benefit and protection of all 
owners of 2021 Bonds, by mandamus or other suit or proceeding at law or  in equity, to enforce its rights 
against the Commission and to compel the Commission and any of its officers, agents or employees to 
perform and carry out their duties under such provisions  of this Agreement; provided, however, that the 
sole remedy for a violation of this Agreement shall be limited to an action to compel specific performance 
of the obligations of the Commission under this Agreem ent and shall not include any rights to monetary 
damages.  This Agreement shall terminate if no 20 21 Bonds remain outstanding (without regard to an 
economic defeasance) or if the provisions of the Rule  concerning continuing disclosure are no longer in 
effect, whichever occurs first. 
 
 5. Amendments.  This Agreement may be  amended, changed or modified by the 
Commission and the Dissemination Agent, without the consent of, or notice to, any owners of the 2021 
Bonds, (a) to comply with or conform to the provis ions of the Rule or any amendments thereto or 
authoritative interpretations thereof by the SEC or its staff (whether required or optional), (b) to add a 
dissemination agent for the informatio n required to be provided pursuant to this Agreement and to make 
any necessary or desirable provisions with respect ther eto, (c) to add to the covenants of the Commission 
for the benefit of the owners of the 2021 Bonds, (d) to modify the contents, presentation and format of the 
annual financial information from time to time as a resu lt of a change in circumstances that arises from a 
change in legal requirements, or (e) to otherwise m odify the undertakings in a manner consistent with the 
provisions of state legislation responding to the requirements of the Rule concerning continuing 
disclosure; provided, however, that in the case of a ny amendment pursuant to clause (d) or (e), (i) the 
undertaking, as amended, would have complied with the requirements of the Rule at the time of the 
offering of the 2021 Bonds, after taking into account a ny amendments or authoritative interpretations of 
the Rule, as well as any change in circumstances, and (ii) the amendment does not materially impair the 
interests of the owners of the 2021 Bonds, as de termined either by a party unaffiliated with the 
Commission (such as Commission bond counsel) or by the vote or consent of the owners of a majority in 
outstanding principal amount of the 2021 Bonds affected thereby at or prior to the time of such 
amendment.  Any amendment, change or modification to this Agreement shall be in writing. 
 
 6. Counterparts.  This Agreement may be ex ecuted in several counterparts, each of which 
shall be an original and all of which shall constitute but one and the same instrument. 
 
 7. Governing Law.  This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in accordance with 
the laws of the Commonwealth and applicable law of the United States of America. 
 
 8. Titles of Sections.  The titles of sections in this Agreement shall have no effect in 
construing this Agreement. 
 
 9. Actions to be Performed on Non-Business Days.  Any action requir ed by this Agreement 
to be taken on a Saturday, Sunday or holiday with in the Commonwealth may be taken on the next 
business day with the same force and effect as if taken on the day so required.
